Support

Product support included

What's Product Support?

In the event your product doesn't work as expected or you need help using it, Amazon offers free product support options such as live phone/chat with an Amazon associate, manufacturer contact information, step-by-step troubleshooting guides, and help videos.

By solving product issues, we help the planet by extending the life of products. Availability of support options differ by product and country. [Learn more](https://www.amazon.com/ps/product-support?ref_=dp_pls_support&ref_=dp_ret_policy)

### Purchase options and add-ons

* * *

- 9-Level Heat Control – Experience steam to your ideal preference with our 2.6L high-capacity steamer, designed with 9 heat levels and remote control. The home sauna warms up in minutes to provide a soothing 130°F, personal spa experience.
- Portable & Spacious – This pop-up personal sauna offers ample room to stretch while sitting comfortably in the included chair. When you're finished, pack it up effortlessly with its collapsible design for convenient storage.
- Robust Design – Made from thick, waterproof polyester, this at home sauna retains heat effectively, with no pungent odors. Plus, our secure sealing prevents steam leakage for a fully immersive sauna experience.
- Therapeutic Benefits – Enjoy steam support, like improved skin tone, muscle relaxation, and boosted immunity. Step into Zen Sweat’s portable steam sauna to feel lighter, clearer, and more energized.
- Complete Sauna Kit – Get everything you need in one package: sauna tent, steamer, foldable chair, waterproof mat, foot massager, remote, and a carrying case. It’s the ultimate indoor sauna kit, made for seamless setup and indulgent comfort.

## From the brand

![Zen Sweat Portable Steam Sauna, At Home Sauna, Pop Up Sauna Design](https://images-na.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/G/01/x-locale/common/grey-pixel.gif)

[_Previous page_](https://www.amazon.com/Zen-Sweat-Portable-Sauna-Home/dp/B0CZC4NSK3#)

2. ![](https://images-na.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/G/01/x-locale/common/grey-pixel.gif)





Not Just Steam. A Smarter Way to Reset.



Zen Sweat started with a simple belief: in a world that won’t slow down, recovery isn’t a luxury — it’s survival.



So we reimagined the at-home sauna — using clean, non-toxic materials, an open, breathable design, and details that don’t cut corners.



No gimmicks. No clones. Just a tool that feels like it was built for you — because it was.

3. ![](https://images-na.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/G/01/x-locale/common/grey-pixel.gif)





Why I Built Zen Sweat



After working in healthcare & respiratory therapy for 5+ years, I’ve seen how powerful steam therapy can be for the body, mind, and mood.



Most options on Amazon felt cheap, complicated, or unrealistic for everyday use. I built Zen Sweat to be different — a safe, high-quality steam sauna you can set up in seconds. No noise. No fluff. Just real recovery that fits into your space.

4. ![Instant Pop Up Sauna Setup, Anti Claustrophia Design](https://images-na.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/G/01/x-locale/common/grey-pixel.gif)

5. ![Because recovery is part of the mission, full body detox 130 degree heat,](https://images-na.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/G/01/x-locale/common/grey-pixel.gif)

6. ![Your Space, Your Pace, Your Life](https://images-na.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/G/01/x-locale/common/grey-pixel.gif)

7. ![Real People, Real Results](https://images-na.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/G/01/x-locale/common/grey-pixel.gif)

8. ![Built different , priced right](https://images-na.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/G/01/x-locale/common/grey-pixel.gif)

9. #### Why Zen Sweat?



To bring real benefits of high-quality steam therapy into every home — safely, simply, and without compromise.







#### What makes it different?



Most saunas you see are the same recycled black box — copy-pasted, mass-produced, and questionably made.



We built Zen Sweat differently. Safer materials. Better design. Real care in every detail — because you’re meant to breathe in this product.







#### What’s the value of something you’ll actually use?

How customer reviews and ratings work

Customer Reviews, including Product Star Ratings help customers to learn more about the product and decide whether it is the right product for them.

To calculate the overall star rating and percentage breakdown by star, we don’t use a simple average. Instead, our system considers things like how recent a review is and if the reviewer bought the item on Amazon. It also analyzed reviews to verify trustworthiness.

[Learn more how customers reviews work on Amazon](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_omni_lm_btn?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)

### Customers say

Customers find the portable sauna heats up beautifully and is easy to set up, with one customer noting it stays over 100 degrees for the entire session. They appreciate its relaxation benefits, with one mentioning it feels like a spa, and its functionality and portability receive positive feedback. Customers like its size, with one noting it fits perfectly in their apartment, and its sturdiness, particularly the included chair and foot massager.

##### Amazing Portable Steam Sauna ! It actually works










Reviewed in the United States on July 30, 2024







I was initially skeptical about portable saunas, but this product completely exceeded my expectations. The setup was incredibly easy and quick—I didn’t even need to refer to the instructions. It includes a chair and a foot massager, making the experience even more enjoyable for added comfort while you relax and enjoy the steam. Despite its compact size, it produces a surprising amount of heat, which really impressed me. I’m thrilled to say that this sauna delivers everything you’d expect from a home sauna and more. I highly recommend it!

##### [_5.0 out of 5 stars_ Packs a Punch!](https://www.amazon.com/gp/customer-reviews/R3VL0AJAIEX70A/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)



Reviewed in the United States on September 25, 2024

[Verified Purchase](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_avp?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)






This Sauna is simply amazing. I always thought these home saunas would be underpowered and a hassle to use but it's very much the opposite. Setup is extremely easy and the mat that goes on the bottom protects from water leaks meaning you can set it up in your home anywhere( I would be careful if you have expensive hardwood, however I used it on my faux hardwood and there was very minimal water leaks so it was totally fine)



The machine it comes with is quite powerful, as someone who uses the steam room a lot, this little thing surprised me with how strong it was. For people with experience I recommend using the maximum setting to get a good sweat. You can also add essential oils directly to the water boiler and that takes the experience to a whole new level.



The cleanup is also extremely easy and this thing packs up into a super thin shape. I took it with me on my trips and it was so amazing to have a steam sauna at a lakeside cottage.

# Product Summary: Portable Sauna for Home \| 2.6L at Home Sauna Steam Tent, Remote, & Foot Massager \| 9 Levels, Pop Up Sauna w/Chair & Waterproof Mat, 4.7' H x 2.6' W at Home Sauna Full Body

From Zen Sweat

## About this Item

- 9-Level Heat Control – Experience steam to your ideal preference with our 2.6L high-capacity steamer, designed with 9 heat levels and remote control. The home sauna warms up in minutes to provide a soothing 130°F, personal spa experience.
- Portable & Spacious – This pop-up personal sauna offers ample room to stretch while sitting comfortably in the included chair. When you're finished, pack it up effortlessly with its collapsible design for convenient storage.
- Robust Design – Made from thick, waterproof polyester, this at home sauna retains heat effectively, with no pungent odors. Plus, our secure sealing prevents steam leakage for a fully immersive sauna experience.
- Therapeutic Benefits – Enjoy steam support, like improved skin tone, muscle relaxation, and boosted immunity. Step into Zen Sweat’s portable steam sauna to feel lighter, clearer, and more energized.
- Complete Sauna Kit – Get everything you need in one package: sauna tent, steamer, foldable chair, waterproof mat, foot massager, remote, and a carrying case. It’s the ultimate indoor sauna kit, made for seamless setup and indulgent comfort.

## Product Description

"Bring the spa home with Zen Sweat’s Portable Sauna, crafted to transform your space into a private wellness retreat. Featuring a full-body steam experience, this at-home sauna allows you to enjoy the relaxing benefits of steam support with no complex setup. Designed with convenience and functionality in mind, the Zen Sweat Sauna includes a 2.6L steamer that quickly heats up to provide a therapeutic steam environment in minutes, complete with 9 adjustable levels and a remote control to personalize your experience. The pop-up design means no assembly tools are required—simply unfold, connect the steamer, and enjoy instant relaxation. This indoor sauna tent also features a spacious, 4.7-foot height and 2.6-foot width, giving you ample room to sit comfortably while enjoying your steam. The package comes complete with essentials, including a foldable chair, a waterproof floor mat, a durable polymer foot massager, and a carrying case, making it a comprehensive setup for home use or even for travel. Well being benefits are at the core of Zen Sweat’s design, offering improved blood circulation, skin rejuvenation, and pressure comfort, all while promoting a more restful sleep experience. Unlike dry saunas, the steam feature offers a gentler heat that promotes deeper relaxation and helps relieve tension more effectively. Our exceptional polyester fabric ensures durability and heat retention without unpleasant odors, while the secure seals around the frame help prevent leaks, allowing you to enjoy your sauna. Zen Sweat’s attention to detail includes a preventive steamer shutoff feature that safeguards against overheating. The added stability in design allows the sauna to be securely used in various home environments. Every element, from the remote control to the secure steam box connection, has been crafted to make Zen Sweat your preferred choice for relaxation and self-care."
